                         Our hope is to share all the comforts and charm of Airbnb: a private room with access to a large yard and a short stroll to our amazing community parks overlooking the bay area. But additionally, the space boasts modern amenities and convenient proximity to both San Francisco and Silicon Valley, being midway between the two and less than a half hour commute to either. So whether you're a visiting professional, family, outdoor enthusiast, or looking for a temporary home while in the Bay Area, this space is ideal for those who are looking for a comfortable retreat with all the conveniences of a real home.
